GT (fixed function of `epsilon, T`):
\[
64.9458\,\epsilon^{0.6137004742}\exp\!\left(-\frac{36.94514734}{8.314\,T}\right)\;-\;0.21482227\,(T-331.6841118)\;+\;3.55398315\,(T-331.6841118)\,\log(\epsilon+1).

Key structural requirements that must hold **simultaneously** for any match:
1) A term of the form \(A\,\epsilon^{0.6137}\exp(-K/T)\) (product of a non-integer power of epsilon and an Arrhenius-in-\(1/T\) exponential).  
2) A **linear-in-\(T\)** term \(-0.2148(T-331.684)\) (i.e., \(-0.2148T + \text{constant}\)).  
3) A **\((T-331.684)\log(\epsilon+1)\)** term (i.e., \(T\log(\epsilon+1)\) plus a \(-331.684\log(\epsilon+1)\) part).  
No candidate can match unless it can generate both (2) and (3) and also the Arrhenius product (1).

### Candidate-by-candidate analysis

1. `T*c0*epsilon + T*c1*exp(c2*epsilon) + ...`
   - Has only polynomial/rational in epsilon and `exp(c2*epsilon)` (exponential in epsilon, not in `1/T`), and no `log(epsilon+1)` multiplied by `(T-const)`.
   - Cannot produce \(\epsilon^{0.6137}\exp(-K/T)\) nor \((T-331.684)\log(\epsilon+1)\). **No match.**

2. `... + c5*sin(c6*log(c7*Abs(epsilon) + 1) + c8) ...`
   - Has `sin(log(...))`, not `log(epsilon+1)` linearly; also no `exp(-K/T)` and no epsilon fractional power. **No match.**

3. `T*c0*log(c1*Abs(epsilon) + 1) + ... + exp(c4*epsilon) + ...`
   - Can make a `T*log(...)` term, but GT needs `(T-331.684)*log(epsilon+1)` which also includes a **non-T** `log(epsilon+1)` term with fixed coefficient \(-331.684*3.5539\). Candidate 3 has no standalone `log(...)` term (only inside `sin` and multiplied by `T`).
   - Also lacks \(\epsilon^{0.6137}\exp(-K/T)\). **No match.**

4. `T*c0*epsilon + ... + sin(log(...))`
   - No Arrhenius `exp(-K/T)`, no linear `log(epsilon+1)` term. **No match.**

5. Similar issues: only powers/rational in epsilon and `sin(log(...))`; no `exp(-K/T)` and no linear `log(epsilon+1)` term. **No match.**

6. `T*c0*log(c1*exp(c2*Abs(epsilon)) + 1) + T*c3 + ...`
   - Log argument depends on epsilon via `exp(c2|epsilon|)`; cannot equal `log(epsilon+1)` for all epsilon by parameter choice.

I need to analyze each candidate against the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT:** `64.95*epsilon^0.614*exp(-36.95/(8.314*T)) - 0.215*(T - 331.68) + 3.554*(T - 331.68)*log(epsilon + 1)`

Let me expand the GT:
- Term 1: `64.95*epsilon^0.614*exp(-4.443/T)` (Arrhenius-like term)
- Term 2: `-0.215*T + 71.31` (linear in T)
- Term 3: `3.554*T*log(epsilon+1) - 1178.6*log(epsilon+1)` (T*log and log terms)

So GT = `64.95*epsilon^0.614*exp(-4.443/T) + 3.554*T*log(epsilon+1) - 0.215*T - 1178.6*log(epsilon+1) + 71.31`

Key basis functions in GT:
1. `epsilon^0.614 * exp(-c/T)` — fractional power of epsilon times Arrhenius
2. `T*log(epsilon+1)` — product of T and log
3. `T` — linear in T
4. `log(epsilon+1)` — logarithmic
5. Constant

Let me check each candidate for these basis functions:
